2328         /**
2329          * Produces a VarHandle giving access to a static field {@code name} of
2330          * type {@code type} declared in a class of type {@code decl}.
2331          * The VarHandle's variable type is {@code type} and it has no
2332          * coordinate types.
2333          * <p>
2334          * Access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup
2335          * class.
2336          * <p>
2337          * If the returned VarHandle is operated on, the declaring class will be
2338          * initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2339          * <p>
2340          * Certain access modes of the returned VarHandle are unsupported under
2341          * the following conditions:
2342          * <ul>
2343          * <li>if the field is declared {@code final}, then the write, atomic
2344          *     update, numeric atomic update, and bitwise atomic update access
2345          *     modes are unsupported.
2346          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code byte},
2347          *     {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int}, {@code long},
2348          *     {@code float}, or {@code double}, then numeric atomic update
2349          *     access modes are unsupported.
2350          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code boolean},
2351          *     {@code byte}, {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int} or
2352          *     {@code long} then bitwise atomic update access modes are
2353          *     unsupported.
2354          * </ul>
2355          * <p>
2356          * If the field is declared {@code volatile} then the returned VarHandle
2357          * will override access to the field (effectively ignore the
2358          * {@code volatile} declaration) in accordance to its specified
2359          * access modes.
2360          * <p>
2361          * If the field type is {@code float} or {@code double} then numeric
2362          * and atomic update access modes compare values using their bitwise
2363          * representation (see {@link Float#floatToRawIntBits} and
2364          * {@link Double#doubleToRawLongBits}, respectively).
2365          * @apiNote
2366          * Bitwise comparison of {@code float} values or {@code double} values,
2367          * as performed by the numeric and atomic update access modes, differ
2368          * from the primitive {@code ==} operator and the {@link Float#equals}
2369          * and {@link Double#equals} methods, specifically with respect to
2370          * comparing NaN values or comparing {@code -0.0} with {@code +0.0}.
2371          * Care should be taken when performing a compare and set or a compare
2372          * and exchange operation with such values since the operation may
2373          * unexpectedly fail.
2374          * There are many possible NaN values that are considered to be
2375          * {@code NaN} in Java, although no IEEE 754 floating-point operation
2376          * provided by Java can distinguish between them.  Operation failure can
2377          * occur if the expected or witness value is a NaN value and it is
2378          * transformed (perhaps in a platform specific manner) into another NaN
2379          * value, and thus has a different bitwise representation (see
2380          * {@link Float#intBitsToFloat} or {@link Double#longBitsToDouble} for more
2381          * details).
2382          * The values {@code -0.0} and {@code +0.0} have different bitwise
2383          * representations but are considered equal when using the primitive
2384          * {@code ==} operator.  Operation failure can occur if, for example, a
2385          * numeric algorithm computes an expected value to be say {@code -0.0}
2386          * and previously computed the witness value to be say {@code +0.0}.
2387          * @param decl the class that declares the static field
2388          * @param name the field's name
2389          * @param type the field's type, of type {@code T}
2390          * @return a VarHandle giving access to a static field
2391          * @throws NoSuchFieldException if the field does not exist
2392          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails, or if the field is not {@code static}
2393          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2394          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2395          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2396          * @since 9
2397          */
2398         public VarHandle findStaticVarHandle(Class<?> decl, String name, Class<?> type) throws NoSuchFieldException, IllegalAccessException {
2399             MemberName getField = resolveOrFail(REF_getStatic, decl, name, type);
2400             MemberName putField = resolveOrFail(REF_putStatic, decl, name, type);
2401             return getFieldVarHandle(REF_getStatic, REF_putStatic, decl, getField, putField);
2402         }
2403 
2404         /**
2405          * Produces an early-bound method handle for a non-static method.
2406          * The receiver must have a supertype {@code defc} in which a method
2407          * of the given name and type is accessible to the lookup class.
2408          * The method and all its argument types must be accessible to the lookup object.
2409          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2410          * without any insertion of an additional receiver parameter.
2411          * The given receiver will be bound into the method handle,
2412          * so that every call to the method handle will invoke the
2413          * requested method on the given receiver.
2414          * <p>
2415          * The returned method handle will have
2416          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2417          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set
2418          * <em>and</em> the trailing array argument is not the only argument.
2419          * (If the trailing array argument is the only argument,
2420          * the given receiver value will be bound to it.)
2421          * <p>
2422          * This is almost equivalent to the following code, with some differences noted below:
2423          * <blockquote><pre>{@code
2424 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
2425 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
2426 ...
2427 MethodHandle mh0 = lookup().findVirtual(defc, name, type);
2428 MethodHandle mh1 = mh0.bindTo(receiver);
2429 mh1 = mh1.withVarargs(mh0.isVarargsCollector());
2430 return mh1;
2431          * }</pre></blockquote>
2432          * where {@code defc} is either {@code receiver.getClass()} or a super
2433          * type of that class, in which the requested method is accessible
2434          * to the lookup class.
2435          * (Unlike {@code bind}, {@code bindTo} does not preserve variable arity.
2436          * Also, {@code bindTo} may throw a {@code ClassCastException} in instances where {@code bind} would
2437          * throw an {@code IllegalAccessException}, as in the case where the member is {@code protected} and
2438          * the receiver is restricted by {@code findVirtual} to the lookup class.)
2439          * @param receiver the object from which the method is accessed
2440          * @param name the name of the method
2441          * @param type the type of the method, with the receiver argument omitted
2442          * @return the desired method handle
2443          * @throws NoSuchMethodException if the method does not exist
2444          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2445          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2446          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2447          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2448          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2449          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2450          * @see MethodHandle#bindTo
2451          * @see #findVirtual
2452          */
2453         public MethodHandle bind(Object receiver, String name, MethodType type) throws NoSuchMethodException, IllegalAccessException {
2454             Class<? extends Object> refc = receiver.getClass(); // may get NPE
2455             MemberName method = resolveOrFail(REF_invokeSpecial, refc, name, type);
2456             MethodHandle mh = getDirectMethodNoRestrictInvokeSpecial(refc, method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2457             if (!mh.type().leadingReferenceParameter().isAssignableFrom(receiver.getClass())) {
2458                 throw new IllegalAccessException("The restricted defining class " +
2459                                                  mh.type().leadingReferenceParameter().getName() +
2460                                                  " is not assignable from receiver class " +
2461                                                  receiver.getClass().getName());
2462             }
2463             return mh.bindArgumentL(0, receiver).setVarargs(method);
2464         }
2465 
2466         /**
2467          * Makes a <a href="MethodHandleInfo.html#directmh">direct method handle</a>
2468          * to <i>m</i>, if the lookup class has permission.
2469          * If <i>m</i> is non-static, the receiver argument is treated as an initial argument.
2470          * If <i>m</i> is virtual, overriding is respected on every call.
2471          * Unlike the Core Reflection API, exceptions are <em>not</em> wrapped.
2472          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2473          * with the receiver type prepended (but only if it is non-static).
2474          * If the method's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2475          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2476          * If <i>m</i> is not public, do not share the resulting handle with untrusted parties.
2477          * <p>
2478          * The returned method handle will have
2479          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2480          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2481          * <p>
2482          * If <i>m</i> is static, and
2483          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the method's class will
2484          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2485          * @param m the reflected method
2486          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected method
2487          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2488          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2489          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2490          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2491          */
2492         public MethodHandle unreflect(Method m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2493             if (m.getDeclaringClass() == MethodHandle.class) {
2494                 MethodHandle mh = unreflectForMH(m);
2495                 if (mh != null)  return mh;
2496             }
2497             if (m.getDeclaringClass() == VarHandle.class) {
2498                 MethodHandle mh = unreflectForVH(m);
2499                 if (mh != null)  return mh;
2500             }
2501             MemberName method = new MemberName(m);
2502             byte refKind = method.getReferenceKind();
2503             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial)
2504                 refKind = REF_invokeVirtual;
2505             assert(method.isMethod());
2506             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2507             Lookup lookup = m.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2508             return lookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(refKind, method.getDeclaringClass(), method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2509         }
2510         private MethodHandle unreflectForMH(Method m) {
2511             // these names require special lookups because they throw UnsupportedOperationException
2512             if (MemberName.isMethodHandleInvokeName(m.getName()))
2513                 return MethodHandleImpl.fakeMethodHandleInvoke(new MemberName(m));
2514             return null;
2515         }
2516         private MethodHandle unreflectForVH(Method m) {
2517             // these names require special lookups because they throw UnsupportedOperationException
2518             if (MemberName.isVarHandleMethodInvokeName(m.getName()))
2519                 return MethodHandleImpl.fakeVarHandleInvoke(new MemberName(m));
2520             return null;
2521         }
2522 
2523         /**
2524          * Produces a method handle for a reflected method.
2525          * It will bypass checks for overriding methods on the receiver,
2526          * <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#equiv">as if called</a> from an {@code invokespecial}
2527          * instruction from within the explicitly specified {@code specialCaller}.
2528          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2529          * with a suitably restricted receiver type prepended.
2530          * (The receiver type will be {@code specialCaller} or a subtype.)
2531          * If the method's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2532          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class,
2533          * as if {@code invokespecial} instruction were being linked.
2534          * <p>
2535          * Before method resolution,
2536          * if the explicitly specified caller class is not identical with the
2537          * lookup class, or if this lookup object does not have
2538          * <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#privacc">private access</a>
2539          * privileges, the access fails.
2540          * <p>
2541          * The returned method handle will have
2542          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2543          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2544          * @param m the reflected method
2545          * @param specialCaller the class nominally calling the method
2546          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected method
2547          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails,
2548          *                                or if the method is {@code static},
2549          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2550          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2551          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2552          */
2553         public MethodHandle unreflectSpecial(Method m, Class<?> specialCaller) throws IllegalAccessException {
2554             checkSpecialCaller(specialCaller, m.getDeclaringClass());
2555             Lookup specialLookup = this.in(specialCaller);
2556             MemberName method = new MemberName(m, true);
2557             assert(method.isMethod());
2558             // ignore m.isAccessible:  this is a new kind of access
2559             return specialLookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(REF_invokeSpecial, method.getDeclaringClass(), method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2560         }
2561 
2562         /**
2563          * Produces a method handle for a reflected constructor.
2564          * The type of the method handle will be that of the constructor,
2565          * with the return type changed to the declaring class.
2566          * The method handle will perform a {@code newInstance} operation,
2567          * creating a new instance of the constructor's class on the
2568          * arguments passed to the method handle.
2569          * <p>
2570          * If the constructor's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2571          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2572          * <p>
2573          * The returned method handle will have
2574          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2575          * the constructor's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2576          * <p>
2577          * If the returned method handle is invoked, the constructor's class will
2578          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2579          * @param c the reflected constructor
2580          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected constructor
2581          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2582          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2583          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2584          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2585          */
2586         public MethodHandle unreflectConstructor(Constructor<?> c) throws IllegalAccessException {
2587             MemberName ctor = new MemberName(c);
2588             assert(ctor.isObjectConstructorOrStaticInitMethod());
2589             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2590             Lookup lookup = c.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2591             if (ctor.isObjectConstructor()) {
2592                 assert(ctor.getReturnType() == void.class);
2593                 return lookup.getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(ctor.getDeclaringClass(), ctor);
2594             } else {
2595                 // static init factory is a static method
2596                 assert(ctor.isMethod() && ctor.getReturnType() == ctor.getDeclaringClass() && ctor.getReferenceKind() == REF_invokeStatic);
2597                 assert(!MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(ctor));  // must not be caller-sensitive
2598                 return lookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(ctor.getReferenceKind(), ctor.getDeclaringClass(), ctor, lookup);
2599             }
2600         }
2601 
2602         /**
2603          * Produces a method handle giving read access to a reflected field.
2604          * The type of the method handle will have a return type of the field's
2605          * value type.
2606          * If the field is {@code static}, the method handle will take no arguments.
2607          * Otherwise, its single argument will be the instance containing
2608          * the field.
2609          * If the {@code Field} object's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2610          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2611          * <p>
2612          * If the field is static, and
2613          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the field's class will
2614          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2615          * @param f the reflected field
2616          * @return a method handle which can load values from the reflected field
2617          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2618          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2619          */
2620         public MethodHandle unreflectGetter(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2621             return unreflectField(f, false);
2622         }
2623 
2624         /**
2625          * Produces a method handle giving write access to a reflected field.
2626          * The type of the method handle will have a void return type.
2627          * If the field is {@code static}, the method handle will take a single
2628          * argument, of the field's value type, the value to be stored.
2629          * Otherwise, the two arguments will be the instance containing
2630          * the field, and the value to be stored.
2631          * If the {@code Field} object's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2632          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2633          * <p>
2634          * If the field is {@code final}, write access will not be
2635          * allowed and access checking will fail, except under certain
2636          * narrow circumstances documented for {@link Field#set Field.set}.
2637          * A method handle is returned only if a corresponding call to
2638          * the {@code Field} object's {@code set} method could return
2639          * normally.  In particular, fields which are both {@code static}
2640          * and {@code final} may never be set.
2641          * <p>
2642          * If the field is {@code static}, and
2643          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the field's class will
2644          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2645          * @param f the reflected field
2646          * @return a method handle which can store values into the reflected field
2647          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails,
2648          *         or if the field is {@code final} and write access
2649          *         is not enabled on the {@code Field} object
2650          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2651          */
2652         public MethodHandle unreflectSetter(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2653             return unreflectField(f, true);
2654         }
2655 
2656         private MethodHandle unreflectField(Field f, boolean isSetter) throws IllegalAccessException {
2657             MemberName field = new MemberName(f, isSetter);
2658             if (isSetter && field.isStatic() && field.isFinal())
2659                 throw field.makeAccessException("static final field has no write access", this);
2660             assert(isSetter
2661                     ? MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(field.getReferenceKind())
2662                     : MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsGetter(field.getReferenceKind()));
2663             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2664             Lookup lookup = f.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2665             return lookup.getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(field.getReferenceKind(), f.getDeclaringClass(), field);
2666         }
2667 
2668         /**
2669          * Produces a VarHandle giving access to a reflected field {@code f}
2670          * of type {@code T} declared in a class of type {@code R}.
2671          * The VarHandle's variable type is {@code T}.
2672          * If the field is non-static the VarHandle has one coordinate type,
2673          * {@code R}.  Otherwise, the field is static, and the VarHandle has no
2674          * coordinate types.
2675          * <p>
2676          * Access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup
2677          * class, regardless of the value of the field's {@code accessible}
2678          * flag.
2679          * <p>
2680          * If the field is static, and if the returned VarHandle is operated
2681          * on, the field's declaring class will be initialized, if it has not
2682          * already been initialized.
2683          * <p>
2684          * Certain access modes of the returned VarHandle are unsupported under
2685          * the following conditions:
2686          * <ul>
2687          * <li>if the field is declared {@code final}, then the write, atomic
2688          *     update, numeric atomic update, and bitwise atomic update access
2689          *     modes are unsupported.
2690          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code byte},
2691          *     {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int}, {@code long},
2692          *     {@code float}, or {@code double} then numeric atomic update
2693          *     access modes are unsupported.
2694          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code boolean},
2695          *     {@code byte}, {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int} or
2696          *     {@code long} then bitwise atomic update access modes are
2697          *     unsupported.
2698          * </ul>
2699          * <p>
2700          * If the field is declared {@code volatile} then the returned VarHandle
2701          * will override access to the field (effectively ignore the
2702          * {@code volatile} declaration) in accordance to its specified
2703          * access modes.
2704          * <p>
2705          * If the field type is {@code float} or {@code double} then numeric
2706          * and atomic update access modes compare values using their bitwise
2707          * representation (see {@link Float#floatToRawIntBits} and
2708          * {@link Double#doubleToRawLongBits}, respectively).
2709          * @apiNote
2710          * Bitwise comparison of {@code float} values or {@code double} values,
2711          * as performed by the numeric and atomic update access modes, differ
2712          * from the primitive {@code ==} operator and the {@link Float#equals}
2713          * and {@link Double#equals} methods, specifically with respect to
2714          * comparing NaN values or comparing {@code -0.0} with {@code +0.0}.
2715          * Care should be taken when performing a compare and set or a compare
2716          * and exchange operation with such values since the operation may
2717          * unexpectedly fail.
2718          * There are many possible NaN values that are considered to be
2719          * {@code NaN} in Java, although no IEEE 754 floating-point operation
2720          * provided by Java can distinguish between them.  Operation failure can
2721          * occur if the expected or witness value is a NaN value and it is
2722          * transformed (perhaps in a platform specific manner) into another NaN
2723          * value, and thus has a different bitwise representation (see
2724          * {@link Float#intBitsToFloat} or {@link Double#longBitsToDouble} for more
2725          * details).
2726          * The values {@code -0.0} and {@code +0.0} have different bitwise
2727          * representations but are considered equal when using the primitive
2728          * {@code ==} operator.  Operation failure can occur if, for example, a
2729          * numeric algorithm computes an expected value to be say {@code -0.0}
2730          * and previously computed the witness value to be say {@code +0.0}.
2731          * @param f the reflected field, with a field of type {@code T}, and
2732          * a declaring class of type {@code R}
2733          * @return a VarHandle giving access to non-static fields or a static
2734          * field
2735          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2736          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2737          * @since 9
2738          */
2739         public VarHandle unreflectVarHandle(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2740             MemberName getField = new MemberName(f, false);
2741             MemberName putField = new MemberName(f, true);
2742             return getFieldVarHandleNoSecurityManager(getField.getReferenceKind(), putField.getReferenceKind(),
2743                                                       f.getDeclaringClass(), getField, putField);
2744         }
2745 
2746         /**
2747          * Cracks a <a href="MethodHandleInfo.html#directmh">direct method handle</a>
2748          * created by this lookup object or a similar one.
2749          * Security and access checks are performed to ensure that this lookup object
2750          * is capable of reproducing the target method handle.
2751          * This means that the cracking may fail if target is a direct method handle
2752          * but was created by an unrelated lookup object.
2753          * This can happen if the method handle is <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#callsens">caller sensitive</a>
2754          * and was created by a lookup object for a different class.
2755          * @param target a direct method handle to crack into symbolic reference components
2756          * @return a symbolic reference which can be used to reconstruct this method handle from this lookup object
2757          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2758          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2759          * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the target is not a direct method handle or if access checking fails
2760          * @throws    NullPointerException if the target is {@code null}
2761          * @see MethodHandleInfo
2762          * @since 1.8
2763          */
2764         public MethodHandleInfo revealDirect(MethodHandle target) {
2765             MemberName member = target.internalMemberName();
2766             if (member == null || (!member.isResolved() &&
2767                                    !member.isMethodHandleInvoke() &&
2768                                    !member.isVarHandleMethodInvoke()))
2769                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("not a direct method handle");
2770             Class<?> defc = member.getDeclaringClass();
2771             byte refKind = member.getReferenceKind();
2772             assert(MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsValid(refKind));
2773             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial && !target.isInvokeSpecial())
2774                 // Devirtualized method invocation is usually formally virtual.
2775                 // To avoid creating extra MemberName objects for this common case,
2776                 // we encode this extra degree of freedom using MH.isInvokeSpecial.
2777                 refKind = REF_invokeVirtual;
2778             if (refKind == REF_invokeVirtual && defc.isInterface())
2779                 // Symbolic reference is through interface but resolves to Object method (toString, etc.)
2780                 refKind = REF_invokeInterface;
2781             // Check SM permissions and member access before cracking.
2782             try {
2783                 checkAccess(refKind, defc, member);
2784                 checkSecurityManager(defc, member);
2785             } catch (IllegalAccessException ex) {
2786                 throw new IllegalArgumentException(ex);
2787             }
2788             if (allowedModes != TRUSTED && member.isCallerSensitive()) {
2789                 Class<?> callerClass = target.internalCallerClass();
2790                 if (!hasFullPrivilegeAccess() || callerClass != lookupClass())
2791                     throw new IllegalArgumentException("method handle is caller sensitive: "+callerClass);
2792             }
2793             // Produce the handle to the results.
2794             return new InfoFromMemberName(this, member, refKind);
2795         }
2796 
2797         /// Helper methods, all package-private.
2798 
2799         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, String name, Class<?> type) throws NoSuchFieldException, IllegalAccessException {
2800             checkSymbolicClass(refc);  // do this before attempting to resolve
2801             Objects.requireNonNull(name);
2802             Objects.requireNonNull(type);
2803             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, new MemberName(refc, name, type, refKind), lookupClassOrNull(),
2804                                             NoSuchFieldException.class);
2805         }
2806 
2807         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, String name, MethodType type) throws NoSuchMethodException, IllegalAccessException {
2808             checkSymbolicClass(refc);  // do this before attempting to resolve
2809             Objects.requireNonNull(name);
2810             Objects.requireNonNull(type);
2811             checkMethodName(refKind, name);  // NPE check on name
2812             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, new MemberName(refc, name, type, refKind), lookupClassOrNull(),
2813                                             NoSuchMethodException.class);
2814         }
2815 
2816         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, MemberName member) throws ReflectiveOperationException {
2817             checkSymbolicClass(member.getDeclaringClass());  // do this before attempting to resolve
2818             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getName());
2819             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getType());
2820             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, member, lookupClassOrNull(),
2821                                             ReflectiveOperationException.class);
2822         }
2823 
2824         MemberName resolveOrNull(byte refKind, MemberName member) {
2825             // do this before attempting to resolve
2826             if (!isClassAccessible(member.getDeclaringClass())) {
2827                 return null;
2828             }
2829             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getName());
2830             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getType());
2831             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrNull(refKind, member, lookupClassOrNull());
2832         }
2833 
2834         void checkSymbolicClass(Class<?> refc) throws IllegalAccessException {
2835             if (!isClassAccessible(refc)) {
2836                 throw new MemberName(refc).makeAccessException("symbolic reference class is not accessible", this);
2837             }
2838         }
2839 
2840         boolean isClassAccessible(Class<?> refc) {
2841             Objects.requireNonNull(refc);
2842             Class<?> caller = lookupClassOrNull();
2843             return caller == null || VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(refc, caller, prevLookupClass, allowedModes);
2844         }
2845 
2846         /** Check name for an illegal leading "&lt;" character. */
2847         void checkMethodName(byte refKind, String name) throws NoSuchMethodException {
2848             // "<init>" can only be invoked via invokespecial or it's a static init factory
2849             if (name.startsWith("<") && refKind != REF_newInvokeSpecial &&
2850                     !(refKind == REF_invokeStatic && name.equals("<init>"))) {
2851                     throw new NoSuchMethodException("illegal method name: " + name);
2852             }
2853         }
2854 
2855         /**
2856          * Find my trustable caller class if m is a caller sensitive method.
2857          * If this lookup object has full privilege access, then the caller class is the lookupClass.
2858          * Otherwise, if m is caller-sensitive, throw IllegalAccessException.
2859          */
2860         Lookup findBoundCallerLookup(MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2861             if (MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(m) && !hasFullPrivilegeAccess()) {
2862                 // Only lookups with full privilege access are allowed to resolve caller-sensitive methods
2863                 throw new IllegalAccessException("Attempt to lookup caller-sensitive method using restricted lookup object");
2864             }
2865             return this;
2866         }
2867 
2868         /**
2869          * Returns {@code true} if this lookup has {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2870          * @return {@code true} if this lookup has {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2871          *
2872          * @deprecated This method was originally designed to test {@code PRIVATE} access
2873          * that implies full privilege access but {@code MODULE} access has since become
2874          * independent of {@code PRIVATE} access.  It is recommended to call
2875          * {@link #hasFullPrivilegeAccess()} instead.
2876          * @since 9
2877          */
2878         @Deprecated(since="14")
2879         public boolean hasPrivateAccess() {
2880             return hasFullPrivilegeAccess();
2881         }
2882 
2883         /**
2884          * Returns {@code true} if this lookup has <em>full privilege access</em>,
2885          * i.e. {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2886          * A {@code Lookup} object must have full privilege access in order to
2887          * access all members that are allowed to the {@linkplain #lookupClass() lookup class}.
2888          *
2889          * @return {@code true} if this lookup has full privilege access.
2890          * @since 14
2891          * @see <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#privacc">private and module access</a>
2892          */
2893         public boolean hasFullPrivilegeAccess() {
2894             return (allowedModes & (PRIVATE|MODULE)) == (PRIVATE|MODULE);
2895         }
2896 
2897         /**
2898          * Perform necessary <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">access checks</a>.
2899          * Determines a trustable caller class to compare with refc, the symbolic reference class.
2900          * If this lookup object has full privilege access, then the caller class is the lookupClass.
2901          */
2902         void checkSecurityManager(Class<?> refc, MemberName m) {
2903             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
2904 
2905             SecurityManager smgr = System.getSecurityManager();
2906             if (smgr == null)  return;
2907 
2908             // Step 1:
2909             boolean fullPowerLookup = hasFullPrivilegeAccess();
2910             if (!fullPowerLookup ||
2911                 !VerifyAccess.classLoaderIsAncestor(lookupClass, refc)) {
2912                 ReflectUtil.checkPackageAccess(refc);
2913             }
2914 
2915             if (m == null) {  // findClass or accessClass
2916                 // Step 2b:
2917                 if (!fullPowerLookup) {
2918                     smgr.checkPermission(SecurityConstants.GET_CLASSLOADER_PERMISSION);
2919                 }
2920                 return;
2921             }
2922 
2923             // Step 2a:
2924             if (m.isPublic()) return;
2925             if (!fullPowerLookup) {
2926                 smgr.checkPermission(SecurityConstants.CHECK_MEMBER_ACCESS_PERMISSION);
2927             }
2928 
2929             // Step 3:
2930             Class<?> defc = m.getDeclaringClass();
2931             if (!fullPowerLookup && defc != refc) {
2932                 ReflectUtil.checkPackageAccess(defc);
2933             }
2934         }
2935 
2936         void checkMethod(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2937             boolean wantStatic = (refKind == REF_invokeStatic);
2938             String message;
2939             if (m.isObjectConstructor())
2940                 message = "expected a method, not a constructor";
2941             else if (!m.isMethod())
2942                 message = "expected a method";
2943             else if (wantStatic != m.isStatic())
2944                 message = wantStatic ? "expected a static method" : "expected a non-static method";
2945             else
2946                 { checkAccess(refKind, refc, m); return; }
2947             throw m.makeAccessException(message, this);
2948         }
2949 
2950         void checkField(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2951             boolean wantStatic = !MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind);
2952             String message;
2953             if (wantStatic != m.isStatic())
2954                 message = wantStatic ? "expected a static field" : "expected a non-static field";
2955             else
2956                 { checkAccess(refKind, refc, m); return; }
2957             throw m.makeAccessException(message, this);
2958         }
2959 
2960         /** Check public/protected/private bits on the symbolic reference class and its member. */
2961         void checkAccess(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2962             assert(m.referenceKindIsConsistentWith(refKind) &&
2963                    MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsValid(refKind) &&
2964                    (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsField(refKind) == m.isField()));
2965             int allowedModes = this.allowedModes;
2966             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
2967             int mods = m.getModifiers();
2968             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods) &&
2969                     refKind == REF_invokeVirtual &&
2970                     m.getDeclaringClass() == Object.class &&
2971                     m.getName().equals("clone") &&
2972                     refc.isArray()) {
2973                 // The JVM does this hack also.
2974                 // (See ClassVerifier::verify_invoke_instructions
2975                 // and LinkResolver::check_method_accessability.)
2976                 // Because the JVM does not allow separate methods on array types,
2977                 // there is no separate method for int[].clone.
2978                 // All arrays simply inherit Object.clone.
2979                 // But for access checking logic, we make Object.clone
2980                 // (normally protected) appear to be public.
2981                 // Later on, when the DirectMethodHandle is created,
2982                 // its leading argument will be restricted to the
2983                 // requested array type.
2984                 // N.B. The return type is not adjusted, because
2985                 // that is *not* the bytecode behavior.
2986                 mods ^= Modifier.PROTECTED | Modifier.PUBLIC;
2987             }
2988             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods) && refKind == REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
2989                 // cannot "new" a protected ctor in a different package
2990                 mods ^= Modifier.PROTECTED;
2991             }
2992             if (Modifier.isFinal(mods) &&
2993                     MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(refKind))
2994                 throw m.makeAccessException("unexpected set of a final field", this);
2995             int requestedModes = fixmods(mods);  // adjust 0 => PACKAGE
2996             if ((requestedModes & allowedModes) != 0) {
2997                 if (VerifyAccess.isMemberAccessible(refc, m.getDeclaringClass(),
2998                                                     mods, lookupClass(), previousLookupClass(), allowedModes))
2999                     return;
3000             } else {
3001                 // Protected members can also be checked as if they were package-private.
3002                 if ((requestedModes & PROTECTED) != 0 && (allowedModes & PACKAGE) != 0
3003                         && VerifyAccess.isSamePackage(m.getDeclaringClass(), lookupClass()))
3004                     return;
3005             }
3006             throw m.makeAccessException(accessFailedMessage(refc, m), this);
3007         }
3008 
3009         String accessFailedMessage(Class<?> refc, MemberName m) {
3010             Class<?> defc = m.getDeclaringClass();
3011             int mods = m.getModifiers();
3012             // check the class first:
3013             boolean classOK = (Modifier.isPublic(defc.getModifiers()) &&
3014                                (defc == refc ||
3015                                 Modifier.isPublic(refc.getModifiers())));
3016             if (!classOK && (allowedModes & PACKAGE) != 0) {
3017                 // ignore previous lookup class to check if default package access
3018                 classOK = (VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(defc, lookupClass(), null, FULL_POWER_MODES) &&
3019                            (defc == refc ||
3020                             VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(refc, lookupClass(), null, FULL_POWER_MODES)));
3021             }
3022             if (!classOK)
3023                 return "class is not public";
3024             if (Modifier.isPublic(mods))
3025                 return "access to public member failed";  // (how?, module not readable?)
3026             if (Modifier.isPrivate(mods))
3027                 return "member is private";
3028             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods))
3029                 return "member is protected";
3030             return "member is private to package";
3031         }
3032 
3033         private void checkSpecialCaller(Class<?> specialCaller, Class<?> refc) throws IllegalAccessException {
3034             int allowedModes = this.allowedModes;
3035             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
3036             if ((lookupModes() & PRIVATE) == 0
3037                 || (specialCaller != lookupClass()
3038                        // ensure non-abstract methods in superinterfaces can be special-invoked
3039                     && !(refc != null && refc.isInterface() && refc.isAssignableFrom(specialCaller))))
3040                 throw new MemberName(specialCaller).
3041                     makeAccessException("no private access for invokespecial", this);
3042         }
3043 
3044         private boolean restrictProtectedReceiver(MemberName method) {
3045             // The accessing class only has the right to use a protected member
3046             // on itself or a subclass.  Enforce that restriction, from JVMS 5.4.4, etc.
3047             if (!method.isProtected() || method.isStatic()
3048                 || allowedModes == TRUSTED
3049                 || method.getDeclaringClass() == lookupClass()
3050                 || VerifyAccess.isSamePackage(method.getDeclaringClass(), lookupClass()))
3051                 return false;
3052             return true;
3053         }
3054         private MethodHandle restrictReceiver(MemberName method, DirectMethodHandle mh, Class<?> caller) throws IllegalAccessException {
3055             assert(!method.isStatic());
3056             // receiver type of mh is too wide; narrow to caller
3057             if (!method.getDeclaringClass().isAssignableFrom(caller)) {
3058                 throw method.makeAccessException("caller class must be a subclass below the method", caller);
3059             }
3060             MethodType rawType = mh.type();
3061             if (caller.isAssignableFrom(rawType.parameterType(0))) return mh; // no need to restrict; already narrow
3062             MethodType narrowType = rawType.changeParameterType(0, caller);
3063             assert(!mh.isVarargsCollector());  // viewAsType will lose varargs-ness
3064             assert(mh.viewAsTypeChecks(narrowType, true));
3065             return mh.copyWith(narrowType, mh.form);
3066         }
3067 
3068         /** Check access and get the requested method. */
3069         private MethodHandle getDirectMethod(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3070             final boolean doRestrict    = true;
3071             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3072             return getDirectMethodCommon(refKind, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3073         }
3074         /** Check access and get the requested method, for invokespecial with no restriction on the application of narrowing rules. */
3075         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodNoRestrictInvokeSpecial(Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3076             final boolean doRestrict    = false;
3077             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3078             return getDirectMethodCommon(REF_invokeSpecial, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3079         }
3080         /** Check access and get the requested method, eliding security manager checks. */
3081         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3082             final boolean doRestrict    = true;
3083             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3084             return getDirectMethodCommon(refKind, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3085         }
3086         /** Common code for all methods; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3087         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodCommon(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method,
3088                                                    boolean checkSecurity,
3089                                                    boolean doRestrict,
3090                                                    Lookup boundCaller) throws IllegalAccessException {
3091             checkMethod(refKind, refc, method);
3092             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3093             if (checkSecurity)
3094                 checkSecurityManager(refc, method);
3095             assert(!method.isMethodHandleInvoke());
3096 
3097             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial &&
3098                 refc != lookupClass() &&
3099                 !refc.isInterface() &&
3100                 refc != lookupClass().getSuperclass() &&
3101                 refc.isAssignableFrom(lookupClass())) {
3102                 assert(!method.getName().equals("<init>"));  // not this code path
3103 
3104                 // Per JVMS 6.5, desc. of invokespecial instruction:
3105                 // If the method is in a superclass of the LC,
3106                 // and if our original search was above LC.super,
3107                 // repeat the search (symbolic lookup) from LC.super
3108                 // and continue with the direct superclass of that class,
3109                 // and so forth, until a match is found or no further superclasses exist.
3110                 // FIXME: MemberName.resolve should handle this instead.
3111                 Class<?> refcAsSuper = lookupClass();
3112                 MemberName m2;
3113                 do {
3114                     refcAsSuper = refcAsSuper.getSuperclass();
3115                     m2 = new MemberName(refcAsSuper,
3116                                         method.getName(),
3117                                         method.getMethodType(),
3118                                         REF_invokeSpecial);
3119                     m2 = IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrNull(refKind, m2, lookupClassOrNull());
3120                 } while (m2 == null &&         // no method is found yet
3121                          refc != refcAsSuper); // search up to refc
3122                 if (m2 == null)  throw new InternalError(method.toString());
3123                 method = m2;
3124                 refc = refcAsSuper;
3125                 // redo basic checks
3126                 checkMethod(refKind, refc, method);
3127             }
3128             DirectMethodHandle dmh = DirectMethodHandle.make(refKind, refc, method, lookupClass());
3129             MethodHandle mh = dmh;
3130             // Optionally narrow the receiver argument to lookupClass using restrictReceiver.
3131             if ((doRestrict && refKind == REF_invokeSpecial) ||
3132                     (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind) && restrictProtectedReceiver(method))) {
3133                 mh = restrictReceiver(method, dmh, lookupClass());
3134             }
3135             mh = maybeBindCaller(method, mh, boundCaller);
3136             mh = mh.setVarargs(method);
3137             return mh;
3138         }
3139         private MethodHandle maybeBindCaller(MemberName method, MethodHandle mh, Lookup boundCaller)
3140                                              throws IllegalAccessException {
3141             if (boundCaller.allowedModes == TRUSTED || !MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(method))
3142                 return mh;
3143 
3144             // boundCaller must have full privilege access.
3145             // It should have been checked by findBoundCallerLookup. Safe to check this again.
3146             if (!boundCaller.hasFullPrivilegeAccess())
3147                 throw new IllegalAccessException("Attempt to lookup caller-sensitive method using restricted lookup object");
3148 
3149             MethodHandle cbmh = MethodHandleImpl.bindCaller(mh, boundCaller.lookupClass);
3150             // Note: caller will apply varargs after this step happens.
3151             return cbmh;
3152         }
3153 
3154         /** Check access and get the requested field. */
3155         private MethodHandle getDirectField(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field) throws IllegalAccessException {
3156             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3157             return getDirectFieldCommon(refKind, refc, field, checkSecurity);
3158         }
3159         /** Check access and get the requested field, eliding security manager checks. */
3160         private MethodHandle getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field) throws IllegalAccessException {
3161             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3162             return getDirectFieldCommon(refKind, refc, field, checkSecurity);
3163         }
3164         /** Common code for all fields; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3165         private MethodHandle getDirectFieldCommon(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field,
3166                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3167             checkField(refKind, refc, field);
3168             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3169             if (checkSecurity)
3170                 checkSecurityManager(refc, field);
3171             DirectMethodHandle dmh = DirectMethodHandle.make(refc, field);
3172             boolean doRestrict = (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind) &&
3173                                     restrictProtectedReceiver(field));
3174             if (doRestrict)
3175                 return restrictReceiver(field, dmh, lookupClass());
3176             return dmh;
3177         }
3178         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandle(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3179                                             Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField)
3180                 throws IllegalAccessException {
3181             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3182             return getFieldVarHandleCommon(getRefKind, putRefKind, refc, getField, putField, checkSecurity);
3183         }
3184         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandleNoSecurityManager(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3185                                                              Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField)
3186                 throws IllegalAccessException {
3187             final boolean checkSecurity = false;
3188             return getFieldVarHandleCommon(getRefKind, putRefKind, refc, getField, putField, checkSecurity);
3189         }
3190         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandleCommon(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3191                                                   Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField,
3192                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3193             assert getField.isStatic() == putField.isStatic();
3194             assert getField.isGetter() && putField.isSetter();
3195             assert MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsStatic(getRefKind) == MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsStatic(putRefKind);
3196             assert MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsGetter(getRefKind) && MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(putRefKind);
3197 
3198             checkField(getRefKind, refc, getField);
3199             if (checkSecurity)
3200                 checkSecurityManager(refc, getField);
3201 
3202             if (!putField.isFinal()) {
3203                 // A VarHandle does not support updates to final fields, any
3204                 // such VarHandle to a final field will be read-only and
3205                 // therefore the following write-based accessibility checks are
3206                 // only required for non-final fields
3207                 checkField(putRefKind, refc, putField);
3208                 if (checkSecurity)
3209                     checkSecurityManager(refc, putField);
3210             }
3211 
3212             boolean doRestrict = (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(getRefKind) &&
3213                                   restrictProtectedReceiver(getField));
3214             if (doRestrict) {
3215                 assert !getField.isStatic();
3216                 // receiver type of VarHandle is too wide; narrow to caller
3217                 if (!getField.getDeclaringClass().isAssignableFrom(lookupClass())) {
3218                     throw getField.makeAccessException("caller class must be a subclass below the method", lookupClass());
3219                 }
3220                 refc = lookupClass();
3221             }
3222             boolean isWriteAllowedOnFinalFields = this.allowedModes == TRUSTED;
3223             return VarHandles.makeFieldHandle(getField, refc, getField.getFieldType(), isWriteAllowedOnFinalFields);
3224         }
3225         /** Check access and get the requested constructor. */
3226         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructor(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor) throws IllegalAccessException {
3227             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3228             return getDirectConstructorCommon(refc, ctor, checkSecurity);
3229         }
3230         /** Check access and get the requested constructor, eliding security manager checks. */
3231         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor) throws IllegalAccessException {
3232             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3233             return getDirectConstructorCommon(refc, ctor, checkSecurity);
3234         }
3235         /** Common code for all constructors; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3236         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructorCommon(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor,
3237                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3238             assert(ctor.isObjectConstructor());
3239             checkAccess(REF_newInvokeSpecial, refc, ctor);
3240             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3241             if (checkSecurity)
3242                 checkSecurityManager(refc, ctor);
3243             assert(!MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(ctor));  // maybeBindCaller not relevant here
3244             return DirectMethodHandle.make(ctor).setVarargs(ctor);
3245         }
3246 
3247         /** Hook called from the JVM (via MethodHandleNatives) to link MH constants:
3248          */
3249         /*non-public*/
3250         MethodHandle linkMethodHandleConstant(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, String name, Object type)
3251                 throws ReflectiveOperationException {
3252             if (!(type instanceof Class || type instanceof MethodType))
3253                 throw new InternalError("unresolved MemberName");
3254             MemberName member = new MemberName(refKind, defc, name, type);
3255             MethodHandle mh = LOOKASIDE_TABLE.get(member);
3256             if (mh != null) {
3257                 checkSymbolicClass(defc);
3258                 return mh;
3259             }
3260             if (defc == MethodHandle.class && refKind == REF_invokeVirtual) {
3261                 // Treat MethodHandle.invoke and invokeExact specially.
3262                 mh = findVirtualForMH(member.getName(), member.getMethodType());
3263                 if (mh != null) {
3264                     return mh;
3265                 }
3266             } else if (defc == VarHandle.class && refKind == REF_invokeVirtual) {
3267                 // Treat signature-polymorphic methods on VarHandle specially.
3268                 mh = findVirtualForVH(member.getName(), member.getMethodType());
3269                 if (mh != null) {
3270                     return mh;
3271                 }
3272             }
3273             MemberName resolved = resolveOrFail(refKind, member);
3274             mh = getDirectMethodForConstant(refKind, defc, resolved);
3275             if (mh instanceof DirectMethodHandle
3276                     && canBeCached(refKind, defc, resolved)) {
3277                 MemberName key = mh.internalMemberName();
3278                 if (key != null) {
3279                     key = key.asNormalOriginal();
3280                 }
3281                 if (member.equals(key)) {  // better safe than sorry
3282                     LOOKASIDE_TABLE.put(key, (DirectMethodHandle) mh);
3283                 }
3284             }
3285             return mh;
3286         }
3287         private boolean canBeCached(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, MemberName member) {
3288             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial) {
3289                 return false;
3290             }
3291             if (!Modifier.isPublic(defc.getModifiers()) ||
3292                     !Modifier.isPublic(member.getDeclaringClass().getModifiers()) ||
3293                     !member.isPublic() ||
3294                     member.isCallerSensitive()) {
3295                 return false;
3296             }
3297             ClassLoader loader = defc.getClassLoader();
3298             if (loader != null) {
3299                 ClassLoader sysl = ClassLoader.getSystemClassLoader();
3300                 boolean found = false;
3301                 while (sysl != null) {
3302                     if (loader == sysl) { found = true; break; }
3303                     sysl = sysl.getParent();
3304                 }
3305                 if (!found) {
3306                     return false;
3307                 }
3308             }
3309             try {
3310                 MemberName resolved2 = publicLookup().resolveOrNull(refKind,
3311                     new MemberName(refKind, defc, member.getName(), member.getType()));
3312                 if (resolved2 == null) {
3313                     return false;
3314                 }
3315                 checkSecurityManager(defc, resolved2);
3316             } catch (SecurityException ex) {
3317                 return false;
3318             }
3319             return true;
3320         }
3321         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodForConstant(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, MemberName member)
3322                 throws ReflectiveOperationException {
3323             if (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsField(refKind)) {
3324                 return getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(refKind, defc, member);
3325             } else if (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsMethod(refKind)) {
3326                 return getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(refKind, defc, member, findBoundCallerLookup(member));
3327             } else if (refKind == REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
3328                 return getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(defc, member);
3329             }
3330             // oops
3331             throw newIllegalArgumentException("bad MethodHandle constant #"+member);
3332         }
3333 
3334         static ConcurrentHashMap<MemberName, DirectMethodHandle> LOOKASIDE_TABLE = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
3335     }

3337     /**
3338      * Produces a method handle constructing arrays of a desired type,
3339      * as if by the {@code anewarray} bytecode.
3340      * The return type of the method handle will be the array type.
3341      * The type of its sole argument will be {@code int}, which specifies the size of the array.
3342      *
3343      * <p> If the returned method handle is invoked with a negative
3344      * array size, a {@code NegativeArraySizeException} will be thrown.
3345      *
3346      * @param arrayClass an array type
3347      * @return a method handle which can create arrays of the given type
3348      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is {@code null}
3349      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code arrayClass} is not an array type
3350      * @see java.lang.reflect.Array#newInstance(Class, int)
3351      * @jvms 6.5 {@code anewarray} Instruction
3352      * @since 9
3353      */
3354     public static MethodHandle arrayConstructor(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {
3355         if (!arrayClass.isArray()) {
3356             throw newIllegalArgumentException("not an array class: " + arrayClass.getName());
3357         }
3358         MethodHandle ani = MethodHandleImpl.getConstantHandle(MethodHandleImpl.MH_Array_newInstance).
3359                 bindTo(arrayClass.getComponentType());
3360         return ani.asType(ani.type().changeReturnType(arrayClass));
3361     }

3364      * Produces a method handle returning the length of an array,
3365      * as if by the {@code arraylength} bytecode.
3366      * The type of the method handle will have {@code int} as return type,
3367      * and its sole argument will be the array type.
3368      *
3369      * <p> If the returned method handle is invoked with a {@code null}
3370      * array reference, a {@code NullPointerException} will be thrown.
3371      *
3372      * @param arrayClass an array type
3373      * @return a method handle which can retrieve the length of an array of the given array type
3374      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is {@code null}
3375      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if arrayClass is not an array type
3376      * @jvms 6.5 {@code arraylength} Instruction
3377      * @since 9
3378      */
3379     public static MethodHandle arrayLength(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {

3381     }

3383     /**
3384      * Produces a method handle giving read access to elements of an array,
3385      * as if by the {@code aaload} bytecode.
3386      * The type of the method handle will have a return type of the array's
3387      * element type.  Its first argument will be the array type,
3388      * and the second will be {@code int}.
3389      *
3390      * <p> When the returned method handle is invoked,
3391      * the array reference and array index are checked.
3392      * A {@code NullPointerException} will be thrown if the array reference
3393      * is {@code null} and an {@code ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException} will be
3394      * thrown if the index is negative or if it is greater than or equal to
3395      * the length of the array.
3396      *
3397      * @param arrayClass an array type
3398      * @return a method handle which can load values from the given array type
3399      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
3400      * @throws  IllegalArgumentException if arrayClass is not an array type
3401      * @jvms 6.5 {@code aaload} Instruction
3402      */
3403     public static MethodHandle arrayElementGetter(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {
3404         return MethodHandleImpl.makeArrayElementAccessor(arrayClass, MethodHandleImpl.ArrayAccess.GET);
3405     }
